        <div class="col-12 text-center text-lg-left mx-auto mx-lg-0 py-8 position-relative" style="top: -5%">
          <h3 class="text-mono f4-mktg text-normal color-fg-muted mb-3"><img alt="GitHub Actions" class="d-inline-block mr-3 position-relative top-1" style="width: 27px;" loading="lazy" src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/modules/site/features/actions-icon-actions.svg" />GitHub Actions</h3>
          <h1 class="h2-mktg mb-3 mx-auto"><span>Automate your workflow</span><br class="actions-hero-text-break"> <span>from</span> <span>idea</span> <span>to</span> <span>production</span></h1>
          <p class="f3-mktg color-fg-muted mb-5 mx-auto mx-lg-0" style="max-width: 520px;">GitHub Actions makes it easy to automate all your software workflows, now with world-class CI/CD. Build, test, and deploy your code right from GitHub. Make code reviews, branch management, and issue triaging work the way you want.</p>

      <div class="col-12 col-sm-10 col-md-8 col-lg-6 mx-auto text-center js-build-in-item build-in-scale-up">
        <h2 class="h4-mktg mb-4">Run a workflow<br>on any GitHub event</h2>
        <p class="f4-mktg color-fg-muted text-left">Kick off workflows with GitHub events like push, issue creation, or a new release. Combine and configure actions for the services you use, built and maintained by the community.</p>
        <p class="f4-mktg color-fg-muted text-left mb-4">Whether you want to build a container, deploy a web service, or automate welcoming new users to your open source projects—there's an action for that. Pair GitHub Packages with Actions to simplify package management, including version updates, fast distribution with our global CDN, and dependency resolution, using your existing GITHUB_TOKEN.</p>
      </div>

        <div class="col-10 col-lg-5 mx-auto mx-lg-0 pt-8 mb-10 mb-lg-0">
          <h2 class="h5-mktg mb-3 text-center text-lg-left">Community-powered workflows</h2>
          <p class="f4-mktg color-fg-muted mb-3">GitHub Actions connects all of your tools to automate every step of your development workflow. Easily deploy to any cloud, create tickets in Jira, or publish a package to npm.</p>
          <p class="f4-mktg color-fg-muted mb-3">Want to venture off the beaten path?  Use the millions of open source libraries available on GitHub to create your own actions. Write them in JavaScript or create a container Action—both can interact with the full GitHub API and any other public API.</p>
        </div>

      </div>

      <h2 class="h5-mktg mb-7 text-center text-lg-left">What our community is saying</h2>


<div class="d-flex gutter gutter-lg-spacious flex-content-stretch flex-wrap mb-8">
    <div class="col-12 col-md-6 col-lg-3 mb-7">
